『言葉も通し゛ない見知らぬ国て゛、何もかも無くして途方に暮れていた僕に』
Knowing I can't speak a lick of the language here, I was at a complete loss.
{end}

『近くて゛寝そへ゛っていた浮浪者風の男達か゛、$話しかけてきました』
Still, I tried striking a conversation with a few homeless-looking guys sitting nearby.

『身ふ゛り手ふ゛りて゛持ち物を盗られてしまった事、たった一枚残った写真を見せ』
I used hand gestures to explain what happened to me, and that all I had to show for myself was this one, single photograph.

『写真の場所まて゛行きたいんた゛か゛、と言っても通し゛るはす゛はなく』

{end}

『トンドまて゛行きたいんた゛か゛、と言っても通し゛るはす゛はなく』
I wanted to go to Tondo, but I had no clear way of explaining that to them.

Just as I'd given up, I muttered, "bahala na," to myself.

And that's when the men cracked up at me!

『そして、僕は彼らと一緒に、あの派手なジプニーという乗り物に乗って』
We were all invited to hitch a ride on this flashy bus called a "jeepney".
{end}

『やっとの事て゛トンド地区まて゛辿り着けました』
Then, at long last, I found myself in the Tondo district.
{end}

『それからか゛すこ゛かったんて゛す』
Things got wild after that...
{end}

『僕、いや彼らの話を聞いて、信し゛られないくらいの人々か゛集まってきて』
Now, I've heard stories about this, but I couldn't believe just how big the crowds were!
{end}

『そう、百人以上はいたんし゛ゃないかな。みんな一生懸命あちこちに連絡して…』
I get it. With well over a hundred people, everyone has to make a living somehow.
{end}

『歓声か゛上か゛り、人垣か゛割れました』
With loud cheers all around, the massive crowd had split itself down the middle.
{end}

『そして、そして…』

It was Maria!
{end}

『その夜、僕たちはマリアか゛ブン・ナ・ブンと言っていた夜の遊園地へ行きました』
That night, we went to the Boon Na Boon Amusement Park that Maria once told me about.
{end}

『義兄さん、マニラのクリスマスの夜は街中か゛イルミネーションにおおわれて、それはそれはきれいて゛す』
Let me tell you, Manila is coated in lights over Christmas, and it's... It's just beautiful.
{end}

『それはまるて゛この国の人たちの心のようて゛す』
Beautiful, like the hearts of all the people here.
{end}

『そして大晦日、街中を賑わせる花火の音と光』
And on New Year's Eve, the sounds and lights coming from the fireworks also fill the city.
{end}

The smoke gets so thick, it'll even obscure the moon!
{end}

『義兄さん』
Hideo...
{end}

I've chosen to stay in the Philippines.
{end}

social status, academic background, wealth...
{end}

I wonder now, how valuable those things actually are.
{end}

『そんなものより、僕にはマリアの宝石のような笑顔か゛一番て゛す』
More than anything else, I value Maria's precious, gem-like smile the very most.
{end}
